         <h2><a href="#instant-server-installation-with-snaps" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-instant-server-installation-with-snaps">

            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Instant Server Installation with Snaps</h2> 
         <p>Install Rocket.Chat in seconds on Linux (Ubuntu and others) with:</p> 
         <pre><code>sudo snap install rocketchat-server
</code></pre> 
         <p><a href="https://uappexplorer.com/snap/ubuntu/rocketchat-server"><img src="https://github.com/Sing-Li/bbug/raw/master/images/ubuntulogo.png" alt="Rocket.Chat Snap is recommended for Linux deployments" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p> 
         <p>Installing snaps is very quick. By running that command you have your full Rocket.Chat server up and running. Snaps are secure. They are isolated with all of their dependencies. Snaps also auto update when we release new versions.</p> 
         <p>Our snap features a built-in reverse proxy that can request and maintain free letsencrypt SSL certificates. You can go from zero to a public-facing SSL-secured Rocket.Chat server in less than 5 minutes.</p> 
         <p>Find out more information about our snaps <a href="https://rocket.chat/docs/installation/manual-installation/ubuntu/snaps/">here</a></p>

         <h1><a href="#about-rocketchat" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-about-rocketchat">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>About Rocket.Chat</h1> 
         <p>Rocket.Chat is a Web Chat Server, developed in JavaScript, using the <a href="https://www.meteor.com/install">Meteor</a> fullstack framework.</p> 
         <p>It is a great solution for communities and companies wanting to privately host their own chat service or for developers looking forward to build and evolve their own chat platforms.</p>

         <blockquote> 
          <p>Self-hosted alternatives to popular cloud services</p> 
         </blockquote> 
         <h2><a href="#features" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-features">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Features</h2> 
         <ul> 
          <li>BYOS (bring your own server)</li> 
          <li>Multiple Rooms</li> 
          <li>Direct Messages</li> 
          <li>Private Groups</li> 
          <li>Public Channels</li> 
          <li>Desktop Notifications</li> 
          <li>Mentions</li> 
          <li>Avatars</li> 
          <li>Markdown</li> 
          <li>Emojis</li> 
          <li>Custom Emojis</li> 
          <li>Reactions</li> 
          <li>One touch Geolocation</li> 
          <li>TeX Math Rendering - inline math typesetting</li> 
          <li>Media Embeds</li> 
          <li>Link Previews</li> 
          <li>Sent Message Edit and Deletion</li> 
          <li>Transcripts / History</li> 
          <li>File Upload / Sharing</li> 
          <li>Scalable file sharing - S3 uploads with CDN downloads</li> 
          <li>Full text search</li> 
          <li>Live chat / Messaging call center</li> 
          <li>LDAP Authentication</li> 
          <li>CAS 1.0, 2.0 support for education institutions and hosting providers worldwide</li> 
          <li>Support for Okta SSO through SAML v2</li> 
          <li>I18n - Supports 22 Languages</li> 
          <li>Hubot Friendly</li> 
          <li>(Beta) Face to Face Video Conferencing (aka WebRTC )</li> 
          <li>(Beta) Multi-users Video Group Chat</li> 
          <li>(Beta) Jitsi integration</li> 
          <li>Audio calls</li> 
          <li>Multi-users Audio Conference</li> 
          <li>Screensharing</li> 
          <li>Drupal 7.x and 8.x Plug-in (both stable and development flavours) (<a href="https://www.drupal.org/project/rocket_chat">download</a> and <a href="https://git.drupal.org/project/rocket_chat.git">source code</a> )</li> 
          <li>XMPP bridge (<a href="https://demo.rocket.chat/channel/general">try it</a>)</li> 
          <li>REST APIs</li> 
          <li>Remote Locations Video Monitoring</li> 
          <li>Native real-time APIs for Microsoft C#, Visual Basic, F# and other .NET supported languages (<a href="https://www.nuget.org/packages/Rocket.Chat.Net/0.0.12-pre">Get it!</a>)</li> 
          <li>API access from <a href="https://metacpan.org/pod/Net::RocketChat">Perl</a> and <a href="https://github.com/baloise/rocket-chat-rest-client">Java</a> (community contributions)</li> 
          <li>Chat-ops powered by Hubot: scalable horizontal app integration (early access)</li> 
          <li>Massively scalable hosting and provisioning (beta testing now)</li> 
          <li>Native Cross-Platform Desktop Application <a href="https://rocket.chat/">Windows, Mac OSX, or Linux</a></li> 
          <li>Mobile app for iPhone, iPad, and iPod touch <a href="https://geo.itunes.apple.com/us/app/rocket.chat/id1028869439?mt=8">Download on AppStore!</a></li> 
          <li>Mobile app for Android phone, tablet, and TV stick <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.konecty.rocket.chat">Available now on Google Play!</a></li> 
          <li>Native Firefox OS Application (also for Desktop Firefox and Firefox for Android!) - <a href="https://rocket.chat/docs/installation/mobile-and-desktop-apps/#native-firefox-os-app">Check the docs page for install instructions</a></li> 
          <li>Sandstorm.io instant Rocket.Chat server <a href="https://apps.sandstorm.io/app/vfnwptfn02ty21w715snyyczw0nqxkv3jvawcah10c6z7hj1hnu0">Now on Sandstorm App Store</a></li> 
          <li>Available on <a href="https://cloudron.io/appstore.html#chat.rocket.cloudronapp">Cloudron Store</a></li>

           </svg></a>Development</h1> 
         <h2><a href="#quick-start-for-code-developers" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-quick-start-for-code-developers">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Quick start for code developers</h2> 
         <p>Prerequisites:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><a href="http://git-scm.com/book/en/v2/Getting-Started-Installing-Git">Git</a></li> 
          <li><a href="https://www.meteor.com/install">Meteor</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>Now just clone and start the app:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell">
          <pre>git clone https://github.com/RocketChat/Rocket.Chat.git
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> Rocket.Chat
meteor npm start</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>If you are not a developer and just want to run the server - see <a href="https://rocket.chat/docs/installation/paas-deployments/">deployment methods</a>.</p> 
         <h2><a href="#branching-model" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-branching-model">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Branching Model</h2> 
         <p>See <a href="https://rocket.chat/docs/developer-guides/branches-and-releases/">Branches and Releases</a>.</p> 
         <p>It is based on <a href="http://nvie.com/posts/a-successful-git-branching-model/">Gitflow Workflow</a>, reference section below is derived from Vincent Driessen at nvie.</p> 
         <p>See also this <a href="https://www.atlassian.com/git/tutorials/comparing-workflows/gitflow-workflow">Git Workflows Comparison</a> for more details.</p> 
         <h2><a href="#translations" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-translations">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Translations</h2> 
         <p>We are experimenting <a href="https://translate.lingohub.com/engelgabriel/rocket-dot-chat/dashboard">Lingohub</a>. If you want to help, send an email to support at rocket.chat to be invited to the translation project.</p> 
         <h2><a href="#community" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-community">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Community</h2> 
         <p>Join thousands of members world-wide 24 x 7 in our <a href="https://demo.rocket.chat">community server</a>. Join the conversation at <a href="https://twitter.com/RocketChatApp">Twitter</a>, <a href="https://www.facebook.com/RocketChatApp">Facebook</a> or <a href="https://plus.google.com/+RocketChatApp">Google Plus</a></p> 
         <h2><a href="#how-to-contribute" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-how-to-contribute">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>How to Contribute</h2> 
         <p>Already a JavaScript developer? Familiar with Meteor? <a href="https://github.com/RocketChat/Rocket.Chat/labels/contrib%3A%20easy">Pick an issue</a>, push a PR and instantly become a member of Rocket.Chat's international contributors community.</p> 
         <p>A lot of work has already gone into Rocket.Chat, but we have much bigger plans for it!</p> 
         <h3><a href="#contributor-license-agreement" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-contributor-license-agreement">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Contributor License Agreement</h3> 
         <p>Please review and sign our CLA at <a href="https://cla-assistant.io/RocketChat/Rocket.Chat">https://cla-assistant.io/RocketChat/Rocket.Chat</a></p> 
         <h1><a href="#credits" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-credits">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Credits</h1>

         <h1><a href="#donate" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-donate">
